SQL> select * from journey;

JOURNEY_ID DOJ       TIME   ROUTE_ID   BUS_CODE                                 
---------- --------- ---- ---------- ----------                                 
         1 02-FEB-18 1400        100          1                                 
         2 03-FEB-18 0600        101          1                                 
         3 02-MAR-18 0830        102          1                                 
         4 03-MAR-18 2130        103          1                                 
         5 03-APR-18 1600        104          2                                 
         6 04-APR-18 1000        105          2                                 

6 rows selected.
//1
SQL> create view jview(j_day,j_time,j_rid)as select DOJ,TIME,ROUTE_ID from journey;

View created.

//2
SQL> update jview set j_day ='20-jan-1998' where j_rid=100;

1 row updated.

//3
SQL> select * from jview;

J_DAY     J_TI      J_RID                                                       
--------- ---- ----------                                                       
20-JAN-98 1400        100                                                       
03-FEB-18 0600        101                                                       
02-MAR-18 0830        102                                                       
03-MAR-18 2130        103                                                       
03-APR-18 1600        104                                                       
04-APR-18 1000        105                                                       

6 rows selected.


//4

SQL> create synonym passenger1 for ticket_detail;

Synonym created.

//5
SQL> select * from passenger1;

 TICKET_NO NAME            S        AGE       FARE                              
---------- --------------- - ---------- ----------                              
         3 Mia             F         15       1680                              
         4 Kalif           M         20       1120                              
         5 John            M         25        800                              
         6 Sins            F         18       1600                              
         1 Sunny           F         37        800                              
         2 Leone           M         32        600                              

6 rows selected.


//6
SQL> create synonym route for br;

Synonym created.


//7
SQL> drop synonym route;

Synonym dropped.




//8
SQL> create index routeindex on br(dist);

Index created.

//9
SQL> drop index routeindex;
Index dropped.

//10
SQL> create sequence ticket1
  2  start with 1
  3  increment by 2
  4  maxvalue 20
  5  minvalue 1;

Sequence created.



 

//11
SQL> insert into ticket values(ticket1.nextval,7,'20-feb-1999','21-oct-2005','1500','che','chennai','mumbai',1,200,100);

1 row created.

//12
SQL> alter sequence ticket1 maxvalue 25;

Sequence altered.
